GRU_breitspurbahn_decisions = {
	GRU_Breitspur_cologne_ddorf_dortmund_hannover_hamburg_decision = {
		icon = GFX_Reichsautobahn

		available = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRU_TRAIN_BUILDING }
			781 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			51 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			57 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			59 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 150
		days_remove = 120

		state_target = yes
		targets = { 781 }
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_provinces = { 587 6570 6469 495 6535 9509 405 3395 6377 }
		}

		modifier = { 
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.05
			industrial_capacity_factory = -0.10
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 6
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GRU_TRAIN_BUILDING
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GRU_Breitspur_cologne_ddorf_dortmund_hannover_hamburg_decision"
			clr_country_flag = GRU_TRAIN_BUILDING
			build_railway = {
				path = { 587 6570 6469 495 6535 9509 405 3395 6377 }
				level = 5
			}
			781 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			51 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			57 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}

	GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time = {
		icon = GFX_roem_time
		
		allowed =  { always = no }
		
        available = {
            hidden_trigger = { always = no }
        }
		visible = { has_country_flag = roem_act_ds_coup }
		
        is_good = no
        selectable_mission = no
        days_mission_timeout = 28

		cancel_trigger = {
		    check_variable = { GRU_Overall_Goebbels_Support > 0.94 }
		}
		cancel_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = volkssturm_nmdvp_infl_95
				remove_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time
			    remove_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_fall
			}
        }
		
        timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = tt_add_infl_10_blackfront
			custom_effect_tooltip = tt_add_rev_5
			custom_effect_tooltip = tt_rebl_time

			every_owned_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
		        	    check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority > 0.95 }
		        	}
					add_to_variable = { BlackFront_Authority = 0.01 }
					add_to_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = -0.01 }
				}

				else_if = {
					limit = {
		        	    OR = {
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.90 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.901 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.902 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.903 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.904 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.905 }

							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.907 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.908 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.909 }

							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.91 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.911 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.912 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.913 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.914 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.915 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.916 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.917 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.918 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.919 }

							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.92 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.921 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.922 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.923 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.924 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.925 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.926 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.927 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.928 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.929 }

							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.93 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.931 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.932 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.933 }

							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.582 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.583 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.584 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.585 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.586 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.587 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.588 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.589 }

							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.59 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.591 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.592 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.593 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.594 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.595 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.596 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.597 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.598 }
							check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = 0.599 }
						}
		        	}
					add_to_variable = { BlackFront_Authority = 0.08 }
					add_to_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = -0.08 }
				}

				else_if = {
					limit = {
		        	    check_variable = { Goebbels_Authority < 0.49 }
		        	}
					add_to_variable = { BlackFront_Authority = 0.10 }
					add_to_variable = { Goebbels_Authority = -0.10 }
				}
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				GRU_clamp_spheres_of_influence = yes
			    GRU_recalculate_variables = yes
			    VS_inf_p_bar = yes
			}

			add_to_variable = {
				var = VS_coup_prss_rev
				value = 0.1
			}
			VS_rev_lvl_up_p_bar = yes

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
			    	limit = {
			    		OR = {
							check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.70 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.70 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.71 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.72 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.73 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.74 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.75 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.76 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.77 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.78 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.79 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.80 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.81 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.82 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.83 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.84 }
						}
			    	}
				    activate_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time
				    add_days_mission_timeout = {
                        mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time
                        days = -7
                    }
			    }
				if = {
			    	limit = {
			    		OR = {
							check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.85 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.86 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.87 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.88 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.89 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.90 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.91 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.92 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.93 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.94 }
						    check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.95 }
							check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.96 }
							check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.97 }
							check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.98 }
							check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 0.99 }
						}
			    	}
				    activate_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time
				    add_days_mission_timeout = {
                        mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time
                        days = -14
                    }
			    }
				if = {
			    	limit = {
			    		NOT = {
							OR = {
			                	check_variable = { GRU_Overall_BlackFront_Support > 0.94 }
			                	check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev_var = 100 }
			                }
						}
			    	}
					activate_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time
			    }
				if = {
			    	limit = {
			    		NOT = {
							check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev = 1 }
						}
			    	}
					activate_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time
			    }
			}
        }
    }
	GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_fall = {
		icon = GFX_decision_BOL_establish_arica_department

		allowed = { always = no }
		
        available = {
            hidden_trigger = { always = no }
        }
		visible = { has_country_flag = roem_act_ds_coup }
		
        is_good = no
        selectable_mission = no
        days_mission_timeout = 300

		fire_only_once = yes

		cancel_trigger = {
		    OR = {
				check_variable = { GRU_Overall_BlackFront_Support > 0.94 }
				check_variable = { VS_coup_prss_rev_var = 100 }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
				news_event = gruothernews.3

				clr_country_flag = roem_act_ds_coup
				set_country_flag = roem_coup
				
				remove_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time
			    remove_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_fall
			}
        }
        timeout_effect = {
			news_event = gruothernews.3

			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = roem_act_ds_coup
				set_country_flag = roem_coup

				remove_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_time
			    remove_mission = GRU_volkssturm_roem_rebl_fall
			}
        }
    }

		cost = 0
		days_remove = 60

		fire_only_once = yes

		available = {
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 1149 }
			has_equipment = { artillery_equipment > 35 }
			has_equipment = { anti_air_equipment > 19 }
			has_equipment = { support_equipment > 69 }
			has_equipment = { motorized_equipment > 39 }
			has_manpower > 13099
		}

		ai_will_do = { factor = 2000 }

		complete_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment	amount = -1150 }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment	amount = -36 }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = anti_air_equipment	amount = -20 }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment	amount = -70 }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = motorized_equipment	amount = -40 }
			add_manpower = -13100
		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = volks_unit_tlp

			hidden_effect = {
				random_owned_state = {
					create_unit = {
						Division = "name = \"91. infantry Volkssturm Division\" Division_template = \"Volkssturm Divisions\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = GRU
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRU_NMDVP_PAN_GERMANISM_RELOADED
			country_exists = DEN
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 0
		days_remove = 7

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 6
		}
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				GRU = {
			    	add_ai_strategy = {
			        	type = prepare_for_war
			        	id = DEN
			        	value = 1000
			        }
					add_ai_strategy = {
		            	type = conquer
		            	id = DEN
		            	value = 1000
		            }
			    }
				DEN = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
			        	type = prepare_for_war
			        	id = GRU
			        	value = 1000
			        }
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GRU_pan_germanism_denmark_decision"
			declare_war_on = { type = annex_everything target = DEN }
		}
	}
